<h2> <span class="mw-headline" id="General_Information">General Information</span></h2>
<div class="wi_body" style="width:100%">
<table border="0">

<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Work Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head" style="width:100%">L'elisir d'amore
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th class="wi_head">Alt<span class="mh555">ernative</span><span class="ms555">.</span> Title
</th>
<td class="wi_head">Melodramma giocoso in due atti
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Composer
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Donizetti,_Gaetano" title="Category:Donizetti, Gaetano">Donizetti, Gaetano</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">I-Catalogue Number</span><span class="ms555">I-Cat. No.</span>
</th>
<td>IGD 24
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Movements/Sections</span><span class="ms555">Mov'ts/Sec's</span>
</th>
<td>2 acts
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Perf<span class="mh555">ormance</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1832-05-12 in Milan, Teatro della Canobbiana
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>First Pub<span class="mh555">lication</span><span class="ms555">.</span>
</th>
<td>1832
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Librettist
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romani,_Felice" title="Category:Romani, Felice">Felice Romani</a> (1788-1865)
<dl><dd>after <a href="/wiki/Category:Scribe,_Eug%C3%A8ne" title="Category:Scribe, Eugène">Eugène Scribe</a> (1791–1861)
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th><span class="mh555">Composer Time Period</span><span class="ms555">Comp. Period</span>
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic" title="Category:Romantic">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Piece Style
</th>
<td><a href="/wiki/Category:Romantic_style" title="Category:Romantic style">Romantic</a>
</td></tr>
<tr>
<th>Instrumentation
</th>
<td>voices, mixed chorus, orchestra <div class="expandline" style="background-color:#E8E8E8;margin-left:0;margin-top:0;padding:0">
<dl><dd><i>Cast</i>
<dl><dd>Nemorino (tenor)<br />Adina (soprano)<br />Belcore (baritone)<br />Dulcarama (bass)<br />Giannetta (soprano)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Mixed Chorus</i> 
<dl><dd>sopranos 1/2, tenors 1/2, basses (SSTTB)
</dd></dl>
</dd><dd><i>Orchestra</i>
<dl><dd>piccolo, 2 flutes, 2 oboes, 2 clarinets, 2 bassoons<br />2 horns, 2 trumpets, 3 trombones, timpani, strings </div>
</dd></dl>
</dd></dl>
</td></tr>
